  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1c45e10f-3142-4e5d-ab2d-cf34e62dd558'

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2337007-brenda?shelf=2016-release">2016-release</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1768275737" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4651481062594296118">Mitch was desperate to help his nephew Peter who was dying from an aggressive form of leukaemia – becoming a drug mule meant the payment would be high; the drugs needed for Peter were priced out of their reach so Mitch thought this was the best way. But on the flight back everything went wrong – he tried to dull the pain of the surgery with alcohol – the results were disastrous. He was arrested on arrival in the city…<br/><br/>Detective Betts was surprised by what he saw in front of him – a young man with</span>
  <span id="freeText4651481062594296118" style="display:none">Mitch was desperate to help his nephew Peter who was dying from an aggressive form of leukaemia – becoming a drug mule meant the payment would be high; the drugs needed for Peter were priced out of their reach so Mitch thought this was the best way. But on the flight back everything went wrong – he tried to dull the pain of the surgery with alcohol – the results were disastrous. He was arrested on arrival in the city…<br /><br />Detective Betts was surprised by what he saw in front of him – a young man with no prior convictions, even a pillar of society; but when he discovered the “why” he understood to a degree. But there was much worse to come in the form of the criminals who had controlled the drug run and Mitch. Not afraid to kill to achieve their own ends, the body count was rising. And when Betts was abducted, his shock at what had happened to him while he was unconscious was profound. What would be the results of this vicious crime spree by these seasoned criminals? <br /><br /><i>Brazen Violations</i> by Aussie author Jonathan Macpherson is a fast paced, gritty and brutally intense thriller which I sped through. I was a little stunned at the abrupt ending but this high octane novel is one for fans of the gruesome, nasty thriller – and not for the faint hearted! Recommended.<br /><br />With thanks to the author for this copy to read in exchange for my honest review.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1795843267" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1795843267" />
    <a title="1-Click Addict Support Group" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22365152-1-click-addict-support-group"><img alt="1-Click Addict Support Group" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1510478539p2/22365152.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1795843267?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="1-Click Addict Support Group" class="user" itemprop="url" name="1-Click Addict Support Group" href="/user/show/22365152-1-click-addict-support-group">1-Click Addict Support Group</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1795843267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6791525449954740876"><i>Brazen Violations</i> was one hell of a wild ride. It felt like one of those movies, you know the kind. You don’t know where it’s going, and you definitely don’t know how it’s going to hold it all together to get there, but there’s so much going on, so much suspense and action that you just don’t care. You couldn’t look away if you wanted to. <br/><br/>The plot was so intense that it required a tremendous amount belief suspension. However, there was so much attention to detail that it made it easy to forget p</span>
  <span id="freeText6791525449954740876" style="display:none"><i>Brazen Violations</i> was one hell of a wild ride. It felt like one of those movies, you know the kind. You don’t know where it’s going, and you definitely don’t know how it’s going to hold it all together to get there, but there’s so much going on, so much suspense and action that you just don’t care. You couldn’t look away if you wanted to. <br /><br />The plot was so intense that it required a tremendous amount belief suspension. However, there was so much attention to detail that it made it easy to forget plausibility and just hold on for the thrills. I was impressed by the character development, as not every thriller takes the time to establish such a strong relationship, even with the bad guys. <br /><br />Reading <i>Brazen Violations</i> felt like watching a campy 90’s action movie, with extreme plot twists, gruesome fight scenes, and a final showdown that deserves to be on the big screen. It felt too big for life, too much to take in, and too much left to end. I desperately hope there will be more! ~ George, 3.5 Stars<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6791525449954740876" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1735387416" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1735387416" />
    <a title="Yulia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58867768-yulia"><img alt="Yulia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1478383133p2/58867768.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1735387416?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Yulia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Yulia" href="/user/show/58867768-yulia">Yulia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1735387416" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10863760357410593429">Exhilarating and intense, this dynamite debut is loaded with thrills and wicked fun!<br/><br/>It is so unique, so refreshingly out-of-the-box, I cannot recommend it highly enough. <br/><br/>The story takes situations we are familiar with, eg crime on the black market, and approaches them from a new, sometimes shocking but constantly engaging angle that makes for rapid page turning.<br/>The characters are easy to feel for, to love and cheer for - the good guys, that is, though even the villains are presented as human, ra</span>
  <span id="freeText10863760357410593429" style="display:none">Exhilarating and intense, this dynamite debut is loaded with thrills and wicked fun!<br /><br />It is so unique, so refreshingly out-of-the-box, I cannot recommend it highly enough. <br /><br />The story takes situations we are familiar with, eg crime on the black market, and approaches them from a new, sometimes shocking but constantly engaging angle that makes for rapid page turning.<br />The characters are easy to feel for, to love and cheer for - the good guys, that is, though even the villains are presented as human, rather than your standard cliches.<br /><br />This book is full of the unexpected - I'm so tired of reading a thriller where you know what is going to happen next! There seems to be a dearth of imagination from writers of this genre. Even the titles of many of them are so cliched (check some of the thrillers in my books) - you just know if they're too lazy to come up with an original title, you can probably expect the writing to be lazy too. <br /><br />I cannot recommend this thriller highly enough. <br /><br />On the downside, there are some horror moments, but if you can stomach Game Of Thrones then you should be fine. <br />Also, it is a little short - 200 pages. I wanted more! The story does feel complete, but I just want to read more about these characters. I would love for this to become a series!<br /><br />A warning if you plan to read this on the bus or train, you'll probably miss your stop!</span>

  <span id="freeText7572161015737723700" style="display:none">This is a fast-paced crime thriller that grabbed my attention from the minute I opened the book until the blazing end. Mitch was very desperate to save his nephew who is dying of leukemia, he sold his belongings as did his sister, but needed more money for a new drug said to be wonderful cure. A new author with interesting thoughts and a well written story. I don't like the quickness of the ending, wishing there was a little more there to find out what happens, but I am definitely interested in reading the next one! <br /> I received a copy of this book from Hidden Gems and author Jonathan Macpherson, who I thank for great story and my ability to leave my thoughts in this review.</span>

<div id="review_1986782429" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1986782429" />
    <a title="Eric" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67381549-eric"><img alt="Eric" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1986782429?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eric" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eric" href="/user/show/67381549-eric">Eric</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34738565-brazen-violations">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1986782429" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10103552392602022634">I’m an English teacher and I needed a replacement for the boring novels my students had been reading during the previous schoolyear. So I browsed goodreads.com to find a book with an interesting story, that was less than 200 pages and had a great review score. I made a list and decided to give Brazen Violations a go. Sure, the story was a tad bit campy and farfetched, but the reviews were excellent and I wanted to avoid books from the literary canon.<br/><br/>Right before the book arrived, I decided to go</span>
  <span id="freeText10103552392602022634" style="display:none">I’m an English teacher and I needed a replacement for the boring novels my students had been reading during the previous schoolyear. So I browsed goodreads.com to find a book with an interesting story, that was less than 200 pages and had a great review score. I made a list and decided to give Brazen Violations a go. Sure, the story was a tad bit campy and farfetched, but the reviews were excellent and I wanted to avoid books from the literary canon.<br /><br />Right before the book arrived, I decided to google the author (yes, I’m a fool for not doing that before I made my purchase). I learned that Brazen Violations is the self-published debut of Jonathan Macpherson: a handsome, blue eyed English teacher. There were no real reviews to be found on the net and I was beginning to suspect that the feedback on Amazon and goodreads.com had been somewhat misleading. Spoiler: it was.<br /><br />Writing a book is very hard. I know because I’ve tried it and every time I reread my draft I was disillusioned as my work of genius turned out to be a poorly written mess. There’s so much you need to get “right” and no manual to guide you through the process. Often I couldn’t put my finger on why my writing was flawed, so I gave up trying because I knew I would never find a publisher and I didn’t see the point in self-publishing a sub-par novel.<br /><br />Jonathan Macpherson chose a different path, which I can respect. If you want to make it as a writer you shouldn’t let anything hold you back. But after reading the book, I can tell you that all these five-star reviews on goodreads have probably been written by people from the author’s entourage. Either that, or they all happen to be easily pleased, because this is anything but a five-star novel. If there is one thing I hate, it’s being played a fool, which is why I decided to write this review.<br /><br />The biggest flaw is that the author constantly gives us information that should have been left unsaid because it is either unimportant or painfully obvious. When the bad guys try to kill the protagonist while he is in the hospital, we read:<br /><br />“The nurse had been working quietly, replacing the fluids on the IV stand. It had been several years since she had handled and IV drip but having done it thousands of times, it was almost second nature. She took the vial from her pocket and added it to the saline solution. The vial contained cyanide.”<br /><br />Read that last sentence with Peter Griffin’s voice and you’ll know just what I’m talking about. <br /><br />We are also treated to the characters’ redundant thoughts. When the bad guy packs a container with “a golden brown substance” the protagonist’s thoughts confirm what we already know: “Heroin, Mitch thought. It really is golden brown.” This “stating of the obvious” is layered with clichés (The darkness was heavy and all around him), repetition (every time the bad guy wants to kill someone we learn that he wants to “limit liabilities”) and poor attempts at humor (“Allegedly my cock is the biggest in the building […] according to your mother”).<br /><br />Every single character is an empty vessel; a cardboard cut-out borrowed from popular culture and glued to mundane background. I never related to any of them. We rarely learn something interesting about their psyche and there is no psychological development whatsoever. The bad guys are supposedly ruthless sociopaths but when the cops get too close, one of them almost gets a heart attack and the other one LITERALLY shits his pants. <br /><br />So the style is crude and the characters are a joke, but what about the plot? I shall not complain about the premise of the novel, because I knew that in advance. However, the development of the plot is so ludicrous, that the author is constantly having to pull strings in order to make all the pieces of the puzzle fit. The over-the-top choices of the characters cascade into a series of implausible events and we can clearly see the hands of the puppet master frantically trying to keep everything under control. Despite all his painfully obvious efforts, Macpherson loses his grip and the ending of the novel is as trivial as it is contrived. <br /><br />I must admit that “Brazen Violations” was an easy read and that I effortlessly read the entire thing from start to finish, despite its many, many flaws. So if you like the summary and you’re just looking for an easy read during the summer holidays, perhaps the 3 dollar kindle version isn’t a terrible waste of money. <br /><br />Just be aware that the flawless ratings are as absurd as the plot of this novel. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10103552392602022634" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2381927977" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2381927977" />
    <a title="Cath" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67667158-cath"><img alt="Cath" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494429150p2/67667158.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2381927977?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cath" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cath" href="/user/show/67667158-cath">Cath</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34738565-brazen-violations">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2381927977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9399745727138838066">A desperate man, Mitch, takes on an illegal and risky task to try and save his nephew, who is suffering from a rare type of leukaemia. It involves going to see the ‘Doc’, who can get illegal drugs you need. The drugs Mitch’s sister requires for her son is very expensive and the hospital won’t pay for it. Doc fits him with a hidden cache and he travels home but it arrested and the cache found.<br/><br/>Now he owes the criminals for the payment of the drugs he needs for his nephew, in full. Mitch is being g</span>
  <span id="freeText9399745727138838066" style="display:none">A desperate man, Mitch, takes on an illegal and risky task to try and save his nephew, who is suffering from a rare type of leukaemia. It involves going to see the ‘Doc’, who can get illegal drugs you need. The drugs Mitch’s sister requires for her son is very expensive and the hospital won’t pay for it. Doc fits him with a hidden cache and he travels home but it arrested and the cache found.<br /><br />Now he owes the criminals for the payment of the drugs he needs for his nephew, in full. Mitch is being guarded in hospital while he recovers from the journey and is being investigated by a straight laced detective called Betts. He wants Mitch to give up the identities of all those involved in the drug transfer, but Mitch believes it wasn’t his fault, so surely, the criminals will still give him the drugs. Naïve Mitch really doesn’t have a clue about these matters.<br /><br />Betts comes to interview Mitch and wants him to give details on all the criminals involved with the drug transfer through Doc. There are threats of kidnapping and chaos at every step. Mitch must try to get out of the hospital as his nephew is looking worse, every day. Betts is taken by the criminals and they install a listening and watching device in his chest, to allow them to see and hear what Mitch and the Mitch are actually saying about the gang.<br /><br />Betts will have to try and outsmart the criminals and find the members of the gang and keep Mitch and his family safe. This book covers some real medical dilemmas that are coming to the front in today’s news – expensive medicines that the hospitals in areas, won’t pay for, leaving parents desperate and willing to do anything to help their child. The other book, Outback Creed, by this author, is also one that has a very realistic background to the story. <br /><br />It makes for a great read and there is always something going on to keep your interest. I have enjoyed reading two of the author’s books and now look forward to some more. I would recommend it to anyone who likes crime thrillers with a realistic twist. Enjoy!<br /><br />I received an ARC copy of this book from Hidden Gems and I have freely given my own opinion of the book above. Some are annoyed with the use of different terminology – but I believe in this day and age that most people know what these words mean or can work it out by the context. Maybe even look the word up if you don’t know it – that’s what I do for any word I’ve never heard of. Most people use either American or British English or a mix of both. Authors come from all around the word, as do their readers, you can never please everyone with which you use.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9399745727138838066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17627664331191898628">Preface: I received a free copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>This novel isn't high art by any means, but it is sort of goofy fun, as long as you can suspend your disbelief. There's a lot of over-the-top silliness and gimmicks and the villains are pretty hacky, but the characters are sympathetic enough for you to want to follow along. You can understand Mitch's motives and root for him to help out his little nephew. Betts is a bit harder to get behind, but he grew on me as time w</span>
  <span id="freeText17627664331191898628" style="display:none">Preface: I received a free copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />This novel isn't high art by any means, but it is sort of goofy fun, as long as you can suspend your disbelief. There's a lot of over-the-top silliness and gimmicks and the villains are pretty hacky, but the characters are sympathetic enough for you to want to follow along. You can understand Mitch's motives and root for him to help out his little nephew. Betts is a bit harder to get behind, but he grew on me as time went on and he became less abrasive. The plot is pretty nonsensical, but chugs along at a decent little clip - you'll never really be bored. It had some neat ideas in it, like the surgeries to smuggle drugs, or the chest camera - none of it is terribly realistic, but fun to watch unfold. The villains are pretty over-the-top, but you can cheer for their demise.<br /><br />If you just want a hammy action-adventure story, this will hit the spot. If you're looking for anything deeper, give it a pass.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2031828027?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J C" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J C" href="/user/show/68680095-j-c">J C</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34738565-brazen-violations">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Crime Fiction Fans</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2031828027" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11967963899046936990">As a crime fiction junky, I was hooked!<br/><br/>Some of the most nerve-wracking scenarios I've come across in years! And intriguing action with real motive attached (as opposed to mindless action, which I find boring).<br/><br/>It's a rare pleasure when you find characters that you like who become criminals with noble intentions. <br/><br/>As for the high-tech aspect, I'd never read/seen anything like it, yet it was absolutely plausible. In fact I wouldn't be at all surprised if this became a reality in the near future. <br/><br/>It'</span>
  <span id="freeText11967963899046936990" style="display:none">As a crime fiction junky, I was hooked!<br /><br />Some of the most nerve-wracking scenarios I've come across in years! And intriguing action with real motive attached (as opposed to mindless action, which I find boring).<br /><br />It's a rare pleasure when you find characters that you like who become criminals with noble intentions. <br /><br />As for the high-tech aspect, I'd never read/seen anything like it, yet it was absolutely plausible. In fact I wouldn't be at all surprised if this became a reality in the near future. <br /><br />It's not for everybody (a tad gruesome in parts, but no more so than say The Silence of The Lambs), but for those hungry for an edgy crime thriller, I highly recommend it.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11967963899046936990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0x9TYvv4gHO/1bdel4x5N05BAnp8EvkiKNa5JHR69lPRTm21RR4fbACgPNtfNYtkcsehe35D5jaZfGL5WZ9hoA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2kL64hZ7z12raQp/8kKKr6Ypgj9Y9/yO8BTpO2g6NmnYE8Q1qJ1QQhQcgfo6+3j8mq8hPlqm45pBvjLmRd+hmg==')})
  }
//]]>
